This will be the state when the member has never subscribed, or when it has\\n32:      * unsubscribed from all topics. While in this state the member can commit offsets but won't\\n33:      * be an active member of the consumer group (no heartbeats sent).\\n34:      */\\n35:     UNSUBSCRIBED,\\n36: \\n37:     /**\\n38:      * Member is attempting to join a consumer group. While in this state, the member will send\\n39:      * heartbeat requests on the interval, with epoch 0, until it gets a response with an epoch > 0\\n40:      * or a fatal failure. A member transitions to this state when it tries to join the group for\\n41:      * the first time with a call to subscribe, or when it has been fenced and tries to re-join.\\n42:      */\\n43:     JOINING,\\n44: \\n45:     /**\\n46:      * Member has received a new target assignment (partitions could have been assigned or\\n47:      * revoked), and it is processing it. This will be the state when the member has never subscribed, or when it has\n32:      * unsubscribed from all topics. While in this state the member can commit offsets but won't\n33:      * be an active member of the consumer group (no heartbeats sent).\n34:      */\n35:     UNSUBSCRIBED,\n36: \n37:     /**\n38:      * Member is attempting to join a consumer group. While in this state, the member will send\n39:      * heartbeat requests on the interval, with epoch 0, until it gets a response with an epoch > 0\n40:      * or a fatal failure. A member transitions to this state when it tries to join the group for\n41:      * the first time with a call to subscribe, or when it has been fenced and tries to re-join.\n42:      */\n43:     JOINING,\n44: \n45:     /**\n46:      * Member has received a new target assignment (partitions could have been assigned or\n47:      * revoked), and it is processing it. While in this state, the member will continue to send\n48:      * heartbeat on the interval, and reconcile the assignment (it will commit offsets if\n49:      * needed, invoke the user callbacks for onPartitionsAssigned or onPartitionsRevoked, and make\n50:      * the new assignment effective). Note that while in this state the member may be trying to\n51:      * resolve metadata for the target assignment, or triggering commits/callbacks if topic names\n52:      * already resolved.\n53:      */\n54:     RECONCILING,\n55: \n56:     /**\n57:      * Member has completed reconciling an assignment received, and stays in this state only until\n58:      * the next heartbeat request is sent out to acknowledge the assignment to the server. This\n59:      * state indicates that the next heartbeat request must be sent without waiting for the\n60:      * heartbeat interval to expire. Note that once the ack is sent, the member could go back to\n61:      * {@link #RECONCILING} if it still has assignment waiting to be reconciled (assignments\n62:      * waiting for metadata, assignments for which metadata was resolved, or new assignments\n63:      * received from the broker)\n64:      */\n65:     ACKNOWLEDGING,\n66: \n67:     /**\n68:      * Member is active in a group and has processed all assignments received. While in this\n69:      * state, the member will send heartbeats on the interval.\n70:      */\n71:     STABLE,\n72: \n73:     /**\n74:      * Member transitions to this state when it receives a {@link Errors#UNKNOWN_MEMBER_ID} or\n75:      * {@link Errors#FENCED_MEMBER_EPOCH} error from the broker, indicating that it has been\n76:      * left out of the group. While in this state, the member will stop sending heartbeats, it\n77:      * will give up its partitions by invoking the user callbacks for onPartitionsLost, and then\n78:      * transition to {@link #JOINING} to re-join the group as a new member.\n79:      */\n80:     FENCED,\n81: \n82:     /**\n83:      * The member transitions to this state before sending a heartbeat to leave the group,\n84:      * While in this state, the member will continue sending heartbeats while it release its\n85:      * assignment calling the user's callback. When callbacks complete, the member will transition\n86:      * out of this state into {@link #LEAVING} to send a heartbeat to leave the group. Note that\n87:      * if leaving due to expired poll timer, the member does not execute any callbacks while in\n88:      * this state and just transitions to {@link #LEAVING} and then {@link #STALE}\n89:      */\n90:     PREPARE_LEAVING,\n91: \n92:     /**\n93:      * Member has committed offsets and releases its assignment, so it stays in this state until\n94:      * the next heartbeat request is sent out with epoch -1 or -2 to effectively leave the group.\n95:      * This state indicates that the next heartbeat request must be sent without waiting for the\n96:      * heartbeat interval to expire.\n97:      */\n98:     LEAVING,\n99: \n100:     /**\n101:      * The member failed with an unrecoverable error received in a heartbeat response. This in an\n102:      * unrecoverable state where the member won't send any requests to the broker and cannot\n103:      * perform any other transition.\n104:      */\n105:     FATAL,\n106: \n107:     /**\n108:      * The member transitions to this state when the poll timer expires, indicating that there\n109:      * hasn't been a call to consumer.poll within the <code>max.poll.interval.ms</code>. While in\n110:      * this state, the member will send a heartbeat to leave the group, invoke the\n111:      * onPartitionsLost callback, and clear its assignments. The member will only transition\n112:      * out of this state on the next application poll event. The member will then transition\n113:      * to JOINING, to rejoin the group.\n114:      */\n115:     STALE;\n116: \n117:     // Valid state transitions\n118:     static {\n119: \n120:         STABLE.previousValidStates = Arrays.asList(JOINING, ACKNOWLEDGING, RECONCILING);\n121: \n122:         RECONCILING.previousValidStates = Arrays.asList(STABLE, JOINING, ACKNOWLEDGING, RECONCILING);\n123: \n124:         ACKNOWLEDGING.previousValidStates = Collections.singletonList(RECONCILING);\n125: \n126:         FATAL.previousValidStates = Arrays.asList(JOINING, STABLE, RECONCILING, ACKNOWLEDGING,\n127:                 PREPARE_LEAVING, LEAVING, UNSUBSCRIBED);\n128: \n129:         FENCED.previousValidStates = Arrays.asList(JOINING, STABLE, RECONCILING, ACKNOWLEDGING,\n130:                 PREPARE_LEAVING, LEAVING);\n131: \n132:         JOINING.previousValidStates = Arrays.asList(FENCED, UNSUBSCRIBED, STALE);\n133: \n134:         PREPARE_LEAVING.previousValidStates = Arrays.asList(JOINING, STABLE, RECONCILING,\n135:                 ACKNOWLEDGING, UNSUBSCRIBED);\n136: \n137:         LEAVING.previousValidStates = Collections.singletonList(PREPARE_LEAVING);\n138: \n139:         UNSUBSCRIBED.previousValidStates = Arrays.asList(PREPARE_LEAVING, LEAVING, FENCED);\n140: \n141:         STALE.previousValidStates = Collections.singletonList(LEAVING);\n142:     }\n143: \n144:     private List<MemberState> previousValidStates;\n145: \n146:     MemberState() {\n147:         this.previousValidStates = new false when the member is preparing to leave the group).\n158:      */\n159:     public boolean canHandleNewAssignment() {\n160:         return MemberState.RECONCILING.getPreviousValidStates().contains(this);\n161:     }\n162: }\n163: The implementation includes two major protocol versions: the classic (JoinGroup/SyncGroup) protocol and the modern (ConsumerGroupHeartbeat) protocol.\\n\\n## Classic Group Protocol State Machine\\n\\nThe classic group state machine is defined in **ClassicGroupState.java** with five states:\\n1. **EMPTY** - Group has no members, lingers until offsets expire\\n2. **PREPARING_REBALANCE** - Group is preparing to rebalance after a join group request\\n3. **COMPLETING_REBALANCE** - Group awaits leader's assignment via SyncGroup\\n4. **STABLE** - Group is stable and members are active\\n5. **DEAD** - Final state before cleanup\\n\\nThe state transitions are validated in **ClassicGroup.java** through the `transitionTo()` method and `assertValidTransition()` method. The transitions follow defined rules (e.g., PREPARING_REBALANCE can transition from STABLE, COMPLETING_REBALANCE, or EMPTY).\\n\\n## Modern Consumer Group Protocol State Machine\\n\\nThe modern consumer group uses:\\n- **ConsumerGroupState** enum in **ConsumerGroup.java** with states: EMPTY, ASSIGNING, RECONCILING, STABLE, DEAD\\n- **MemberState** enum in **modern/MemberState.java** with member-level states: STABLE, UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS, UNRELEASED_PARTITIONS, UNKNOWN\\n\\nThe reconciliation logic is implemented in **CurrentAssignmentBuilder.java**, which encapsulates the reconciliation engine that converges member state with target assignment state.\\n\\n## Streams Group Protocol State Machine\\n\\nStreams groups are defined in **StreamsGroup.java** and **streams/MemberState.java**, implementing similar state management for stream processing topology assignments.\\n\\n## Client-Side State Machine\\n\\nThe client-side member state machine is defined in **clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/MemberState.java** with states: UNSUBSCRIBED, JOINING, RECONCILING, ACKNOWLEDGING, STABLE, FENCED, PREPARE_LEAVING, LEAVING, FATAL, STALE.\\n\\n## Main Coordinator Components\\n\\nThe state machine is managed through:\\n- **GroupMetadataManager.java** - The implementation includes two major protocol versions: the classic (JoinGroup/SyncGroup) protocol and the modern (ConsumerGroupHeartbeat) protocol.\\n\\n## Classic Group Protocol State Machine\\n\\nThe classic group state machine is defined in **ClassicGroupState.java** with five states:\\n1. **EMPTY** - Group has no members, lingers until offsets expire\\n2. **PREPARING_REBALANCE** - Group is preparing to rebalance after a join group request\\n3. **COMPLETING_REBALANCE** - Group awaits leader's assignment via SyncGroup\\n4. **STABLE** - Group is stable and members are active\\n5. **DEAD** - Final state before cleanup\\n\\nThe state transitions are validated in **ClassicGroup.java** through the `transitionTo()` method and `assertValidTransition()` method. The transitions follow defined rules (e.g., PREPARING_REBALANCE can transition from STABLE, COMPLETING_REBALANCE, or EMPTY).\\n\\n## Modern Consumer Group Protocol State Machine\\n\\nThe modern consumer group uses:\\n- **ConsumerGroupState** enum in **ConsumerGroup.java** with states: EMPTY, ASSIGNING, RECONCILING, STABLE, DEAD\\n- **MemberState** enum in **modern/MemberState.java** with member-level states: STABLE, UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS, UNRELEASED_PARTITIONS, UNKNOWN\\n\\nThe reconciliation logic is implemented in **CurrentAssignmentBuilder.java**, which encapsulates the reconciliation engine that converges member state with target assignment state.\\n\\n## Streams Group Protocol State Machine\\n\\nStreams groups are defined in **StreamsGroup.java** and **streams/MemberState.java**, implementing similar state management for stream processing topology assignments.\\n\\n## Client-Side State Machine\\n\\nThe client-side member state machine is defined in **clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/MemberState.java** with states: UNSUBSCRIBED, JOINING, RECONCILING, ACKNOWLEDGING, STABLE, FENCED, PREPARE_LEAVING, LEAVING, FATAL, STALE.\\n\\n## Main Coordinator Components\\n\\nThe state machine is managed through:\\n- **GroupMetadataManager.java** - The implementation includes two major protocol versions: the classic (JoinGroup/SyncGroup) protocol and the modern (ConsumerGroupHeartbeat) protocol.\\n\\n## Classic Group Protocol State Machine\\n\\nThe classic group state machine is defined in **ClassicGroupState.java** with five states:\\n1. **EMPTY** - Group has no members, lingers until offsets expire\\n2. **PREPARING_REBALANCE** - Group is preparing to rebalance after a join group request\\n3. **COMPLETING_REBALANCE** - Group awaits leader's assignment via SyncGroup\\n4. **STABLE** - Group is stable and members are active\\n5. **DEAD** - Final state before cleanup\\n\\nThe state transitions are validated in **ClassicGroup.java** through the `transitionTo()` method and `assertValidTransition()` method. The transitions follow defined rules (e.g., PREPARING_REBALANCE can transition from STABLE, COMPLETING_REBALANCE, or EMPTY).\\n\\n## Modern Consumer Group Protocol State Machine\\n\\nThe modern consumer group uses:\\n- **ConsumerGroupState** enum in **ConsumerGroup.java** with states: EMPTY, ASSIGNING, RECONCILING, STABLE, DEAD\\n- **MemberState** enum in **modern/MemberState.java** with member-level states: STABLE, UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS, UNRELEASED_PARTITIONS, UNKNOWN\\n\\nThe reconciliation logic is implemented in **CurrentAssignmentBuilder.java**, which encapsulates the reconciliation engine that converges member state with target assignment state.\\n\\n## Streams Group Protocol State Machine\\n\\nStreams groups are defined in **StreamsGroup.java** and **streams/MemberState.java**, implementing similar state management for stream processing topology assignments.\\n\\n## Client-Side State Machine\\n\\nThe client-side member state machine is defined in **clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/MemberState.java** with states: UNSUBSCRIBED, JOINING, RECONCILING, ACKNOWLEDGING, STABLE, FENCED, PREPARE_LEAVING, LEAVING, FATAL, STALE.\\n\\n## Main Coordinator Components\\n\\nThe state machine is managed through:\\n- **GroupMetadataManager.java** - Contains `classicGroupJoin()`, `classicGroupSync()`, and `consumerGroupHeartbeat()` methods that orchestrate state transitions\\n- **GroupCoordinatorShard.java** - Request handler interface\\n- **GroupCoordinatorService.java** - Service layer for coordinator operations\\n- **GroupCoordinator.java** - Top-level coordinator interface\\n- **GroupCoordinatorRecordHelpers.java** - Helper functions for creating coordinator records\\n\\n## Target Assignment Builders\\n\\nThe assignment process uses:\\n- **TargetAssignmentBuilder.java** (modern consumer and streams) - Builds target assignments for groups\\n- **ShareGroupAssignmentBuilder.java** - For share groups\\n\\nThe Join, Sync, and Rebalance operations are implemented through the interaction of these components, with state transitions recorded as CoordinatorRecords in the __consumer_offsets topic.\"\n}\n","numLines":49,"startLine":1,"totalLines":49}}}
